The **DefaultResourceEncodingConfig** struct (line 42-47) manages resource-specific encoding overrides via SetResourceEncoding(), allowing fine-grained control over storage versions.\\n\\n## Storage Factory and Configuration Chain\\nThe configuration chain begins at **pkg/kubeapiserver/default_storage_factory_builder.go** in NewStorageFactoryConfig() (line 63-91), which establishes ResourceEncodingOverrides for resources that must be stored in non-latest versions. **pkg/registry/admissionregistration/rest/storage_apiserver.go** - Registers admission registration APIs with v1Storage, v1beta1Storage, and v1alpha1Storage for webhook configurations and admission policies.\\n\\nThese providers implement the RESTStorageProvider interface pattern, where NewRESTStorage() orchestrates calls to version-specific storage methods and populates
